# Liberian National Port Authority
company_LNPA = {
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/company_icons/historical_company_icons/LNPA.png"
	background = "gfx/interface/icons/company_icons/company_backgrounds/comp_illu_harbor_shipbuilding.dds"
	
	flavored_company = yes
	
	building_types = {  
		building_shipyards
		building_military_shipyards
		building_motor_industry
	}
	
	potential = {
		has_interest_marker_in_region = region_senegal
	}
	
	attainable = {
		hidden_trigger = { # Hide attainable if it's always fulfilled by possible
			any_scope_state = {
				state_region = s:STATE_LIBERIA
			}
		}
	}
	
	possible = {
		any_scope_state = {
			state_region = s:STATE_LIBERIA
			is_incorporated = yes
			any_scope_building = {
				OR = {
					is_building_type = building_shipyards
					is_building_type = building_military_shipyards
				}
				level >= 3
			}
		}
		has_technology_researched = gantry_cranes
	}
	
	prosperity_modifier = {
		unit_navy_defense_mult = 0.05
		unit_navy_offense_mult = 0.05
	}	
	
	ai_weight = {
		value = 3 # Higher base value for flavored companies
	}
}

# United Fruit Company
company_united_fruit = {
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/company_icons/historical_company_icons/american_united_fruit_co.dds"
	background = "gfx/interface/icons/company_icons/company_backgrounds/comp_illu_plantation.dds"

	flavored_company = yes

	building_types = {
		building_banana_plantation
		building_sugar_plantation
	}

	potential = {
		OR = {
			country_has_primary_culture = cu:yankee
			country_has_primary_culture = cu:dixie
		}
	}

	possible = {
		OR = {
			any_scope_state = {
				OR = {
					state_is_in_south_america = yes
					state_is_in_central_america = yes
				}
				any_scope_building = {
					is_building_type = building_banana_plantation
					level >= 5
				}
			}
		}
		any_subject_or_below = {
			OR = {
				country_is_in_south_america = yes
				country_is_in_central_america = yes
			}
			any_scope_state = {
				any_scope_building = {
					is_building_type = building_banana_plantation
					level >= 3
				}
			}
		}
	}

	prosperity_modifier = {
		building_group_bg_plantations_throughput_add = 0.2
		country_infamy_decay_mult = -0.25
	}

	ai_weight = {
		value = 3 # Higher base value for flavored companies
	}
}

company_caribbean_petroleum = {
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/company_icons/historical_company_icons/venezuela_caribbean_petroleum_company.dds"
	background = "gfx/interface/icons/company_icons/company_backgrounds/comp_illu_oil_drills.dds"
	
	flavored_company = yes
	
	building_types = {
		building_oil_rig
	}
	
	potential = {
		has_interest_marker_in_region = region_gran_colombia
	}
	
	attainable = {
		hidden_trigger = { # Hide attainable if it's always fulfilled by possible
			any_scope_state = {
				OR = {
					state_region = s:STATE_ZULIA
					state_region = s:STATE_MIRANDA
				}
			}
		}
	}	
	
	possible = {
		any_scope_state = {
			OR = {
				state_region = s:STATE_ZULIA
				state_region = s:STATE_MIRANDA
			}
			is_incorporated = yes
			any_scope_building = {
				is_building_type = building_oil_rig
				level >= 5
			}
		}
		has_technology_researched = pumpjacks
	}
	
	prosperity_modifier = {
		country_convoys_capacity_mult = 0.2
		interest_group_ig_industrialists_approval_add = 2
		interest_group_ig_industrialists_pop_attraction_mult = 0.1
	}
	
	ai_weight = {
		value = 3 # Higher base value for flavored companies
	}
}

		building_arms_industry
		building_munition_plants
	}

	potential = {
		has_interest_marker_in_region = region_italy
	}

	attainable = {
		hidden_trigger = { # Hide attainable if it's always fulfilled by possible
			any_scope_state = {
				state_region = s:STATE_PIEDMONT
			}
		}
	}

	possible = {
		any_scope_state = {
			state_region = s:STATE_PIEDMONT
			is_incorporated = yes
			any_scope_building = {
				is_building_type = building_arms_industry
				level >= 3
			}
		}
		has_technology_researched = bolt_action_rifles
	}

	prosperity_modifier = {

		building_motor_industry_throughput_add = 0.1

company_great_indian_railway = {
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/company_icons/historical_company_icons/india_great_indian_peninsula_railway.dds"
	background = "gfx/interface/icons/company_icons/company_backgrounds/comp_illu_railways.dds"

	flavored_company = yes

	building_types = {
		building_railway
	}

	potential = {
		OR = {
			has_interest_marker_in_region = region_south_india
			has_interest_marker_in_region = region_north_india
		}
	}

	attainable = {
		hidden_trigger = { # Hide attainable if it's always fulfilled by possible
			any_scope_state = {
				OR = {
					region = sr:region_south_india
					region = sr:region_north_india
				}
				is_incorporated = yes
			}
		}
	}

	possible = {
		any_scope_state = {
			OR = {
				region = sr:region_south_india
				region = sr:region_north_india
			}
			is_incorporated = yes
			has_building = building_railway
			count >= 3
		}
	}

	prosperity_modifier = {
		state_infrastructure_from_population_add = 0.5
		state_infrastructure_from_population_max_add = 20
	}

	ai_weight = {
		value = 3 # Higher base value for flavored companies
	}
}

# Tata
company_tata = {
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/company_icons/historical_company_icons/india_tata.dds"
	background = "gfx/interface/icons/company_icons/company_backgrounds/comp_illu_manufacturing_heavy.dds"

	flavored_company = yes

	building_types = {
		building_textile_mills
		building_steel_mills
	}

	potential = {
		has_interest_marker_in_region = region_south_india
	}

	attainable = {
		hidden_trigger = { # Hide attainable if it's always fulfilled by possible
			any_scope_state = {
				state_region = s:STATE_BOMBAY
			}
		}
	}

	possible = {
		any_scope_state = {
			state_region = s:STATE_BOMBAY
			is_incorporated = yes
			any_scope_building = {
				OR = {
					is_building_type = building_textile_mills
					is_building_type = building_steel_mills
				}
				level >= 5
			}
		}
	}

	prosperity_modifier = {
		building_construction_sector_throughput_add = 0.05
		country_max_weekly_construction_progress_add = 10
	}

	ai_weight = {
		value = 3 # Higher base value for flavored companies
	}
}

# Calcutta and Burma Steamship Navigation Company
company_CaBSNC = {
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/company_icons/basic_shipyards.dds"
	background = "gfx/interface/icons/company_icons/company_backgrounds/comp_illu_harbor_shipbuilding.dds"

	flavored_company = yes

	building_types = {
		building_shipyards
		building_trade_center
	}

	potential = {
		OR = {
			has_interest_marker_in_region = region_south_india
			has_interest_marker_in_region = region_north_india
			has_interest_marker_in_region = region_indochina
		}
	}

	attainable = {
		hidden_trigger = { # Hide attainable if it's always fulfilled by possible
			any_scope_state = {
				OR = {
			       state_region = s:STATE_SOUTH_BENGAL
			       state_region = s:STATE_PEGU
			    }
			}
		}
	}

	possible = {
		any_scope_state = {
		    OR = {
			state_region = s:STATE_SOUTH_BENGAL
			state_region = s:STATE_PEGU
			}
			is_incorporated = yes
			any_scope_building = {
				OR = {
					is_building_type = building_shipyards
					is_building_type = building_port
				}
				level >= 3
			}
		}
	}

	prosperity_modifier = {
		building_trade_center_throughput_add = 0.1
		unit_army_offense_mult = 0.05
	}

	ai_weight = {
		value = 3 # Higher base value for flavored companies
	}
}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/company_icons/historical_company_icons/egyptian_rail.dds"
	background = "gfx/interface/icons/company_icons/company_backgrounds/comp_illu_railways.dds"
	
	flavored_company = yes
	
	building_types = { 
		building_railway
	}
	
	potential = {
		country_has_primary_culture = cu:misri
	}		

	possible = { 
		any_scope_state = {
			region = sr:region_nile_basin
			is_incorporated = yes
			has_building = building_railway
			count >= 4
		}
		has_technology_researched = corporate_charters			
	}
	
	prosperity_modifier = {
		state_infrastructure_from_population_max_add = 20
		market_land_trade_capacity_add = 10
	}	
	
	ai_weight = {
		value = 3 # Higher base value for flavored companies
	}
}

# Suez Canal Company
company_suez_company = {
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/company_icons/historical_company_icons/suez_company.dds"
	background = "gfx/interface/icons/company_icons/company_backgrounds/comp_illu_harbor_shipbuilding.dds"
	
	flavored_company = yes
	
	building_types = {
		building_trade_center
		building_shipyards
		building_military_shipyards
	}
	
	potential = {
		has_interest_marker_in_region = region_nile_basin
	}
	
	attainable = {
		hidden_trigger = { # Hide attainable if it's always fulfilled by possible
			any_scope_state = {
				state_region = s:STATE_SINAI
			}
		}
	}	

	possible = {
		any_scope_state = {
			state_region = s:STATE_SINAI
			any_scope_building = {
				is_building_type = building_suez_canal
				occupancy >= 0.5
			}
		}
	}
	
	prosperity_modifier = {
		country_trade_route_competitiveness_mult = 0.25
		country_tax_income_add = 50000
	}
	
	ai_weight = {
		value = 3 # Higher base value for flavored companies
	}
}

	background = "gfx/interface/icons/company_icons/company_backgrounds/comp_illu_farm_wheat.dds"

	flavored_company = yes

	building_types = {
		building_food_industry
		building_wheat_farm #herbs
	}

	potential = {
		has_interest_marker_in_region = region_danubia
	}

	attainable = {
		hidden_trigger = { # Hide attainable if it's always fulfilled by possible
			any_scope_state = {
				state_region = s:STATE_CENTRAL_HUNGARY
			}
		}
	}

	possible = {
		any_scope_state = {
			state_region = s:STATE_CENTRAL_HUNGARY
			is_incorporated = yes
			any_scope_building = {
				is_building_type = building_food_industry
				level >= 3
			}
		}
	}

	prosperity_modifier = {
		state_mortality_wealth_mult = -0.001
        state_radicals_from_sol_change_mult = -0.075
	}

	ai_weight = {
		value = 3 # Higher base value for flavored companies
	}
}

# Bunge & Born
company_bunge_born = {
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/company_icons/historical_company_icons/argentina_bunge_y_born.dds"
	background = "gfx/interface/icons/company_icons/company_backgrounds/comp_illu_farm_wheat.dds"
	
	flavored_company = yes
	
	building_types = {
		building_wheat_farm
		building_maize_farm
		building_food_industry
	}
	
	potential = {
		has_interest_marker_in_region = region_la_plata
		OR = {
		country_has_primary_culture = cu:platinean
		country_has_primary_culture = cu:argentine
		}
	}
	
	attainable = {
		hidden_trigger = { # Hide attainable if it's always fulfilled by possible
			any_scope_state = {
				region = sr:region_la_plata
				is_incorporated = yes
			}
		}
	}		
	
	possible = {
		any_scope_state = {
			region = sr:region_la_plata
			is_incorporated = yes
			any_scope_building = {
				OR = {
					is_building_type = building_wheat_farm
					is_building_type = building_maize_farm
				}
				level >= 3
			}
			count >= 4
		}
	}
	
	prosperity_modifier = {
		interest_group_ig_rural_folk_pop_attraction_mult = 0.2
		building_tooling_workshops_throughput_add = 0.075
	}
	
	ai_weight = {
		value = 3 # Higher base value for flavored companies
	}
}

# Compañía Sudamericana de Vapores (Chile)
company_sudamericana_de_vapores = {
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/company_icons/historical_company_icons/chile_csav.dds"
	background = "gfx/interface/icons/company_icons/company_backgrounds/comp_illu_harbor_shipbuilding.dds"
	
	building_types = {  
		building_trade_center
		building_shipyards
	}
	
	potential = {
		has_dlc_feature = rp1_content
		has_interest_marker_in_region = region_la_plata
	}
	
	attainable = {
		hidden_trigger = { # Hide attainable if it's always fulfilled by possible
			any_scope_state = {
				state_region = s:STATE_SANTIAGO
			}
		}
	}		

	possible = {
		any_scope_state = {
			state_region = s:STATE_SANTIAGO
			is_incorporated = yes
			any_scope_building = {
				is_building_type = building_port
				level >= 3
			}
		}
		has_technology_researched = screw_frigate
	}
	
	prosperity_modifier = {
		state_colony_growth_speed_mult = 0.1
		country_convoys_capacity_mult = 0.1
	}
	
	ai_weight = {
		value = 3 # Higher base value for flavored companies
	}
}

# Córdoba Central Railway
company_cordoba_railway = {
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/company_icons/historical_company_icons/argentina_cordoba_cenral_railway.dds"
	background = "gfx/interface/icons/company_icons/company_backgrounds/comp_illu_railways.dds"
	
	building_types = {  
		building_railway
	}
	
	potential = {
		has_dlc_feature = rp1_content
		has_interest_marker_in_region = region_la_plata
	}
	
	attainable = {
		hidden_trigger = { # Hide attainable if it's always fulfilled by possible
			any_scope_state = {
				state_region = s:STATE_LA_PAMPA
			}
		}
	}		

	possible = {
		any_scope_state = {
			state_region = s:STATE_LA_PAMPA
			is_incorporated = yes
			has_building = building_railway
		}
		any_scope_state = {
			has_state_trait = state_trait_pampas
			is_incorporated = yes
			has_building = building_railway
			count >= 2
		}
	}
	
	prosperity_modifier = {
		building_wheat_farm_throughput_add = 0.1
		building_livestock_ranch_throughput_add = 0.1
	}
	
	ai_weight = {
		value = 3 # Higher base value for flavored companies
	}
}

# Tandanor / Talleres Navales de Marina
company_Tandanor = {
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/company_icons/historical_company_icons/TANDANOR.png"
	background = "gfx/interface/icons/company_icons/company_backgrounds/comp_illu_harbor_shipbuilding.dds"
	
	flavored_company = yes
	
	building_types = {
		building_shipyards
		building_military_shipyards
	}
	
	potential = {
		has_interest_marker_in_region = region_la_plata
	}
	
	attainable = {
		hidden_trigger = { # Hide attainable if it's always fulfilled by possible
			any_scope_state = {
				state_region = s:STATE_BUENOS_AIRES
			}
		}
	}		
	
	possible = {
		any_scope_state = {
			state_region = s:STATE_BUENOS_AIRES
			is_incorporated = yes
			any_scope_building = {
					is_building_type = building_military_shipyards
				level >= 3
			}
		}
	}
	
	prosperity_modifier = {
		unit_navy_defense_mult = 0.1
	}
	
	ai_weight = {
		value = 3 # Higher base value for flavored companies
	}
}
